	<h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">Prince Andrew, Duke of York</h1>

<p><b>Prince Andrew, Duke of York</b>, <span class="noexcerpt" style="font-size:100%;"><a href="/wiki/Knight_of_the_Order_of_the_Garter" class="mw-redirect" title="Knight of the Order of the Garter">KG</a><span style="font-size:14px;">&#44;</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Knight_Grand_Cross_of_the_Royal_Victorian_Order" class="mw-redirect" title="Knight Grand Cross of the Royal Victorian Order">GCVO</a><span style="font-size:14px;">&#44;</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Canadian_Forces_Decoration" class="mw-redirect" title="Canadian Forces Decoration">CD</a><span style="font-size:14px;">&#44;</span>&#32;<a href="/wiki/Personal_aide-de-camp" title="Personal aide-de-camp">ADC(P)</a></span> (Andrew Albert Christian Edward, born 19 February 1960) is a member of the <a href="/wiki/British_royal_family" title="British royal family">British royal family</a>. He is the third child and second son of <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Queen Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prince_Philip,_Duke_of_Edinburgh" title="Prince Philip, Duke of Edinburgh">Prince Philip, Duke of Edinburgh</a>. At the time of his birth, he was second in the <a href="/wiki/Succession_to_the_British_throne" title="Succession to the British throne">line of succession to the British throne</a>; as of May&#160;2019<sup class="plainlinks noexcerpt noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;"><a class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Prince_Andrew,_Duke_of_York&amp;action=edit">&#91;update&#93;</a></sup>, he is eighth in line.
</p><p>He holds the rank of <a href="/wiki/Commander_(Royal_Navy)" title="Commander (Royal Navy)">commander</a> and the honorary rank of <a href="/wiki/Vice_admiral_(Royal_Navy)" class="mw-redirect" title="Vice admiral (Royal Navy)">vice admiral</a> (as of February 2015) in the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a>, in which he served as an active-duty helicopter pilot and instructor and as the captain of a warship. He saw active service during the <a href="/wiki/Falklands_War" title="Falklands War">Falklands War</a>, flying on multiple missions including <a href="/wiki/Anti-surface_warfare" title="Anti-surface warfare">anti-surface warfare</a>, <a href="/wiki/Exocet_missile" class="mw-redirect" title="Exocet missile">Exocet missile</a> decoy, and casualty evacuation.
</p><p>In 1986, Prince Andrew married <a href="/wiki/Sarah,_Duchess_of_York" title="Sarah, Duchess of York">Sarah Ferguson</a>; the couple's marriage, separation and eventual divorce in 1996 attracted a high level of media coverage. As well as carrying out various official engagements, he served as Britain's <a href="/wiki/Special_Representative_for_International_Trade_and_Investment" title="Special Representative for International Trade and Investment">Special Representative for International Trade and Investment</a> until July 2011.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Early_life_and_education">Early life and education</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg/220px-G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="165" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg/330px-G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8c/G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg/440px-G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3648" data-file-height="2736" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:G_House_from_the_South_Lawn_on_an_Autumn_Afternoon.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Gordonstoun</div></div></div>
<p>Prince Andrew was born in the Belgian Suite of <a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> on 19 February 1960,<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> the third child and second son of <a href="/wiki/Queen_Elizabeth_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Queen Elizabeth II">Queen Elizabeth II</a> and <a href="/wiki/Prince_Philip,_Duke_of_Edinburgh" title="Prince Philip, Duke of Edinburgh">Prince Philip, Duke of Edinburgh</a>. He was baptised in the Palace's Music Room on 8 April 1960 by the <a href="/wiki/Archbishop_of_Canterbury" title="Archbishop of Canterbury">Archbishop of Canterbury</a>, <a href="/wiki/Geoffrey_Fisher" title="Geoffrey Fisher">Geoffrey Fisher</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;b&#93;</a></sup> He is the namesake of his paternal grandfather, <a href="/wiki/Prince_Andrew_of_Greece_and_Denmark" title="Prince Andrew of Greece and Denmark">Prince Andrew of Greece and Denmark</a>, who died 16 years before he was born.
</p><p>Prince Andrew was the first child born to a reigning monarch since the birth in 1857 of <a href="/wiki/Queen_Victoria" title="Queen Victoria">Queen Victoria</a>'s youngest child, <a href="/wiki/Princess_Beatrice_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Princess Beatrice of the United Kingdom">Princess Beatrice</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> As with his older siblings, Andrew was looked after by a <a href="/wiki/Governess" title="Governess">governess</a>, who was responsible for his early education at Buckingham Palace.<sup id="cite_ref-Trade-ED_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trade-ED-7">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He was sent to <a href="/wiki/Heatherdown_School" title="Heatherdown School">Heatherdown School</a> near <a href="/wiki/Ascot,_Berkshire" title="Ascot, Berkshire">Ascot</a> in <a href="/wiki/Berkshire" title="Berkshire">Berkshire</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Heat-Lake_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Heat-Lake-8">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> In September 1973, he entered <a href="/wiki/Gordonstoun" title="Gordonstoun">Gordonstoun</a>, in northern <a href="/wiki/Scotland" title="Scotland">Scotland</a>, which his father and elder brother had also attended.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> While there, he spent six months‚Äîfrom January to June 1977‚Äîparticipating in an exchange programme to <a href="/wiki/Lakefield_College_School" title="Lakefield College School">Lakefield College School</a> in <a href="/wiki/Canada" title="Canada">Canada</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Heat-Lake_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Heat-Lake-8">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-DoY-Ed_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoY-Ed-10">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> He left Gordonstoun in July two years later with <a href="/wiki/Advanced_Level_(UK)" class="mw-redirect" title="Advanced Level (UK)">A-Levels</a><sup id="cite_ref-DoY-Ed_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-DoY-Ed-10">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> in English, history, economics, and political science. He did not go to university but instead entered the <a href="/wiki/Britannia_Royal_Naval_College" title="Britannia Royal Naval College">Britannia Royal Naval College</a> at <a href="/wiki/Dartmouth,_Devon" title="Dartmouth, Devon">Dartmouth</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Military_service">Military service</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Royal_Navy">Royal Navy</span></h3>
<p>The Royal Household announced in November 1978 that Prince Andrew would join the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Navy" title="Royal Navy">Royal Navy</a> the following year. In December he underwent various sporting tests and examinations at the <a href="/wiki/Officer_and_Aircrew_Selection_Centre" title="Officer and Aircrew Selection Centre">Aircrew Selection Centre</a>, at <a href="/wiki/London_Biggin_Hill_Airport" title="London Biggin Hill Airport">RAF Biggin Hill</a>, along with further tests and interviews at <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Lee-on-Solent_(HMS_Daedalus)" title="RNAS Lee-on-Solent (HMS Daedalus)">HMS <i>Daedalus</i></a>, and interviews at the <a href="/wiki/Admiralty_Interview_Board" title="Admiralty Interview Board">Admiralty Interview Board</a>, <a href="/wiki/HMS_Sultan_(establishment)" title="HMS Sultan (establishment)">HMS <i>Sultan</i></a>. During March and April 1979, the prince was enrolled at the Royal Naval College Flight, undergoing pilot training, until he was accepted as a trainee helicopter pilot and signed on for 12 years from 11 May 1979. On 1 September of the same year, Prince Andrew was appointed as a <a href="/wiki/Midshipman" title="Midshipman">midshipman</a>, and entered <a href="/wiki/Britannia_Royal_Naval_College" title="Britannia Royal Naval College">Britannia Royal Naval College</a>, Dartmouth.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> During 1980 he also took the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Marines" title="Royal Marines">Royal Marines</a> <a href="/wiki/All_Arms_Commando_Course" title="All Arms Commando Course">All Arms Commando Course</a>.
</p><p>After passing out from Dartmouth, the prince went on to elementary flying training with the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Air_Force" title="Royal Air Force">Royal Air Force</a> at <a href="/wiki/RAF_Leeming" title="RAF Leeming">RAF Leeming</a>, and later, basic flying training with the navy at <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Culdrose_(HMS_Seahawk)" title="RNAS Culdrose (HMS Seahawk)">HMS <i>Seahawk</i></a>, where he learned to fly the <a href="/wiki/A%C3%A9rospatiale_Gazelle" title="A√©rospatiale Gazelle">Gazelle</a> helicopter.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> After being awarded his wings, he moved onto more advanced training on the <a href="/wiki/Westland_Sea_King" title="Westland Sea King">Sea King</a> helicopter, and conducted operational flying training until 1982. He joined carrier-based squadron, <a href="/wiki/820_Naval_Air_Squadron" title="820 Naval Air Squadron">820 Naval Air Squadron</a>, serving aboard the <a href="/wiki/Aircraft_carrier" title="Aircraft carrier">aircraft carrier</a>, <a href="/wiki/HMS_Invincible_(R05)" title="HMS Invincible (R05)">HMS <i>Invincible</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Falklands_War">Falklands War</span></h3>
<p>The <a href="/wiki/Falkland_Islands" title="Falkland Islands">Falkland Islands</a>, which are a <a href="/wiki/British_overseas_territory" class="mw-redirect" title="British overseas territory">British overseas territory</a> claimed by <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> were <a href="/wiki/1982_invasion_of_the_Falkland_Islands" title="1982 invasion of the Falkland Islands">invaded</a> by Argentina on 2 April 1982, an event that instigated the <a href="/wiki/Falklands_War" title="Falklands War">Falklands War</a>. <i>Invincible</i> was one of the two operational aircraft carriers available at the time, and, as such, was to play a major role in the <a href="/wiki/British_naval_forces_in_the_Falklands_War" title="British naval forces in the Falklands War">Royal Navy task force</a> assembled to sail south to retake the islands.
</p><p>Prince Andrew's place on board and the possibility of the Queen's son being killed in action made the British Government apprehensive, and the Cabinet desired that Prince Andrew be moved to a desk job for the duration of the conflict. The Queen, though, insisted that her son be allowed to remain with his ship.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> Prince Andrew remained on board <i>Invincible</i> to serve as a Sea King helicopter co-pilot, flying on missions that included <a href="/wiki/Anti-submarine_warfare" title="Anti-submarine warfare">anti-submarine warfare</a> and <a href="/wiki/Anti-Surface_Warfare" class="mw-redirect" title="Anti-Surface Warfare">anti-surface warfare</a>, <a href="/wiki/Exocet_missile" class="mw-redirect" title="Exocet missile">Exocet missile</a> decoy, casualty evacuation, transport, and search and air rescue.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He witnessed the Argentinian attack on the <a href="/wiki/SS_Atlantic_Conveyor" title="SS Atlantic Conveyor">SS <i>Atlantic Conveyor</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the cessation of the war, <i>Invincible</i> returned to <a href="/wiki/Portsmouth" title="Portsmouth">Portsmouth</a>, where the Queen and Prince Philip joined other families of the crew in welcoming the vessel home. The <a href="/wiki/National_Reorganization_Process" title="National Reorganization Process">Argentine military government</a> reportedly planned, but did not attempt, to assassinate the prince on <a href="/wiki/Mustique" title="Mustique">Mustique</a> in July 1982.<sup id="cite_ref-reuters19831017_19-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-reuters19831017-19">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> Though he had brief assignments to <a href="/wiki/HMS_Illustrious_(R06)" title="HMS Illustrious (R06)">HMS <i>Illustrious</i></a>, <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Culdrose_(HMS_Seahawk)" title="RNAS Culdrose (HMS Seahawk)">RNAS Culdrose</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Joint_Services_School_of_Intelligence" title="Joint Services School of Intelligence">Joint Services School of Intelligence</a>, Prince Andrew remained with <i>Invincible</i> until 1983. Commander <a href="/wiki/Nigel_Ward" class="mw-redirect" title="Nigel Ward">Nigel Ward</a>'s memoir, <i>Sea Harrier Over the Falklands</i>, described Prince Andrew as "an excellent pilot and a very promising officer."<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Following his return from the Falklands War and until his marriage to Sarah Ferguson, Prince Andrew dated actress <a href="/wiki/Koo_Stark" title="Koo Stark">Koo Stark</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_naval_officer">Career naval officer</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg/220px-Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="146" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg/330px-Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3c/Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg/440px-Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg 2x" data-file-width="4256" data-file-height="2832" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Prince_Andrew_and_Leon_E._Panetta.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Duke of York with the US <a href="/wiki/Secretary_of_Defense" class="mw-redirect" title="Secretary of Defense">Secretary of Defense</a> <a href="/wiki/Leon_Panetta" title="Leon Panetta">Leon Panetta</a> commemorating the 100th anniversary of Naval Aviation at the <a href="/wiki/National_Building_Museum" title="National Building Museum">National Building Museum</a> in 2011</div></div></div>
<p>In late 1983, Prince Andrew transferred to <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Portland" class="mw-redirect" title="RNAS Portland">RNAS Portland</a>, was trained to fly the <a href="/wiki/Westland_Lynx" title="Westland Lynx">Lynx</a> helicopter, and was promoted to the rank of <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant#Lieutenant" title="Lieutenant">Lieutenant</a> on 1 February 1984, whereupon the Queen appointed him as her personal <a href="/wiki/Aide-de-Camp" class="mw-redirect" title="Aide-de-Camp">aide-de-Camp</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Prince Andrew served aboard <a href="/wiki/HMS_Brazen_(F91)" title="HMS Brazen (F91)">HMS <i>Brazen</i></a> as a flight pilot until 1986,<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> including deployment to the <a href="/wiki/Mediterranean_Sea" title="Mediterranean Sea">Mediterranean Sea</a> as part of <a href="/wiki/Standing_NRF_Maritime_Group_2" class="mw-redirect" title="Standing NRF Maritime Group 2">Standing NRF Maritime Group 2</a>. He undertook the Lieutenants' <a href="/wiki/Royal_Naval_College,_Greenwich" title="Royal Naval College, Greenwich">Greenwich</a> Staff course. On 23 October 1986, the Duke of York (as he was by then) transferred to the <a href="/wiki/General_List" class="mw-redirect" title="General List">General List</a>, enrolled in a four-month helicopter warfare instructor's course at <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Yeovilton_(HMS_Heron)" title="RNAS Yeovilton (HMS Heron)">RNAS Yeovilton</a>, and, upon graduation, served from February 1987 to April 1988 as a helicopter warfare officer in <a href="/wiki/702_Naval_Air_Squadron" title="702 Naval Air Squadron">702 Naval Air Squadron</a>, <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Portland_(HMS_Osprey)" title="RNAS Portland (HMS Osprey)">RNAS Portland</a>. He also served on <a href="/wiki/HMS_Edinburgh_(D97)" title="HMS Edinburgh (D97)">HMS <i>Edinburgh</i></a> as an <a href="/wiki/Watchstanding" class="mw-redirect" title="Watchstanding">Officer of the Watch</a> and Assistant Navigating Officer until 1989, including a six-month deployment as part of exercise <i>Outback 88</i> to the Far East.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Duke of York served as flight commander and pilot of the Lynx HAS3 on <a href="/wiki/HMS_Campbeltown_(F86)" title="HMS Campbeltown (F86)">HMS <i>Campbeltown</i></a> from 1989 to 1991, during which he also acted as Force Aviation Officer to <a href="/wiki/Standing_NRF_Maritime_Group_1" class="mw-redirect" title="Standing NRF Maritime Group 1">Standing NRF Maritime Group 1</a> while <i>Campbeltown</i> was flagship of the <a href="/wiki/NATO" title="NATO">NATO</a> force in the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">North Atlantic</a> from 1990 to 1991.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He passed the squadron command examination on 16 July 1991, attended the <a href="/wiki/Staff_College,_Camberley" title="Staff College, Camberley">Staff College, Camberley</a>, the following year, and completed the Army Staff course. He was promoted to <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_commander_(Royal_Navy)" title="Lieutenant commander (Royal Navy)">Lieutenant-Commander</a> on 1 February and passed the ship command examination on 12 March 1992. From 1993 to 1994, Prince Andrew commanded the Hunt-class <a href="/wiki/Minehunter" title="Minehunter">minehunter</a> <a href="/wiki/HMS_Cottesmore_(M32)" title="HMS Cottesmore (M32)">HMS <i>Cottesmore</i></a>.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>From 1995 to 1996, the Duke was posted as Senior Pilot of <a href="/wiki/815_Naval_Air_Squadron" title="815 Naval Air Squadron">815 Naval Air Squadron</a>, then the largest flying unit in the <a href="/wiki/Fleet_Air_Arm" title="Fleet Air Arm">Fleet Air Arm</a>. His main responsibility was to supervise flying standards and to guarantee an effective operational capability.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> He was promoted to <a href="/wiki/Commander#Royal_Navy" title="Commander">Commander</a> on 27 April 1999,<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> finishing his active naval career at the <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(United_Kingdom)" title="Ministry of Defence (United Kingdom)">British Ministry of Defence</a> in 2001, as an officer of the Diplomatic Directorate of the Naval Staff. In July of that year, the Duke of York was retired from the Active List of the Navy.<sup id="cite_ref-naval_12-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-naval-12">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> Three years later, he was made an Honorary <a href="/wiki/Captain_(Royal_Navy)" title="Captain (Royal Navy)">Captain</a>, rather than the <a href="/wiki/Substantive_rank" class="mw-redirect" title="Substantive rank">substantive rank</a> of Captain, as would be customary. On 19 February 2010, his 50th birthday, he was promoted to Honorary <a href="/wiki/Rear_Admiral_(Royal_Navy)" class="mw-redirect" title="Rear Admiral (Royal Navy)">Rear Admiral</a>. Five years later, he was promoted to Honorary <a href="/wiki/Vice_Admiral_(Royal_Navy)" class="mw-redirect" title="Vice Admiral (Royal Navy)">Vice Admiral</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Relationship_with_Koo_Stark">Relationship with Koo Stark</span></h3>
<p>Prince Andrew met <a href="/wiki/Koo_Stark" title="Koo Stark">Koo Stark</a> in February 1981, and they were close for some two years, before and after his active service in the <a href="/wiki/Falklands_War" title="Falklands War">Falklands War</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-rebuttal_23-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rebuttal-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Tina_Brown" title="Tina Brown">Tina Brown</a> has claimed that this was Andrew's only serious love interest.<sup id="cite_ref-brown_25-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-brown-25">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In October 1982, they took a holiday together on the island of <a href="/wiki/Mustique" title="Mustique">Mustique</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Lady_Colin_Campbell" title="Lady Colin Campbell">Lady Colin Campbell</a>, Andrew was in love, and the Queen was "much taken with the elegant, intelligent, and discreet Koo".<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> However, in 1983, they split up, under pressure from press, paparazzi, and palace.<sup id="cite_ref-rebuttal_23-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rebuttal-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-brown_25-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-brown-25">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> In 1997, Andrew became godfather to Stark's daughter,<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> and in 2015, when Andrew was facing accusations from Virginia Roberts over his connection to <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_Epstein" title="Jeffrey Epstein">Jeffrey Epstein</a>, Stark came to his defence, stating that he was a good man and she could help to rebut the claims.<sup id="cite_ref-rebuttal_23-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-rebuttal-23">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Marriage_to_Sarah_Ferguson">Marriage to Sarah Ferguson</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/Wedding_of_Prince_Andrew_and_Sarah_Ferguson" title="Wedding of Prince Andrew and Sarah Ferguson">Wedding of Prince Andrew and Sarah Ferguson</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House,1988.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House%2C1988.jpg/220px-The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House%2C1988.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="140" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House%2C1988.jpg/330px-The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House%2C1988.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/68/The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House%2C1988.jpg/440px-The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House%2C1988.jpg 2x" data-file-width="3000" data-file-height="1906" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Duke_and_Duchess_of_York_at_Parliament_House,1988.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Andrew and Sarah with <a href="/wiki/Queensland" title="Queensland">Queensland</a> Premier <a href="/wiki/Mike_Ahern_(Australian_politician)" title="Mike Ahern (Australian politician)">Mike Ahern</a>, Brisbane, 1988</div></div></div>
<p>Prince Andrew married <a href="/wiki/Sarah,_Duchess_of_York" title="Sarah, Duchess of York">Sarah Ferguson</a> at <a href="/wiki/Westminster_Abbey" title="Westminster Abbey">Westminster Abbey</a> on 23 July 1986. The same day, the Queen created him <a href="/wiki/Duke_of_York" title="Duke of York">Duke of York</a>, <a href="/wiki/Earl_of_Inverness" title="Earl of Inverness">Earl of Inverness</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Baron_Killyleagh" title="Baron Killyleagh">Baron Killyleagh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> The first two of these titles were previously held by both his maternal <a href="/wiki/George_VI" title="George VI">grandfather</a> and <a href="/wiki/George_V" title="George V">great-grandfather</a>. Prince Andrew had known Ferguson since childhood; they had met occasionally at <a href="/wiki/Polo" title="Polo">polo</a> matches, and became re-acquainted with each other at <a href="/wiki/Royal_Ascot" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Ascot">Royal Ascot</a> in 1985.<sup id="cite_ref-WP-86_30-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WP-86-30">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The couple appeared to have a happy marriage and had two daughters together, presenting a united outward appearance during the late 1980s. His wife's personal qualities were seen as refreshing in the context of the formal protocol surrounding the Royal Family. However, the Duke of York's frequent travel due to his military career, as well as relentless, often critical, media attention focused on the Duchess of York, led to fractures in the marriage. On 19 March 1992, the couple announced plans to separate and did so in an amicable way.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Some months later, pictures appeared in the <a href="/wiki/Tabloid_journalism" title="Tabloid journalism">tabloid</a> media of the Duchess in intimate association with John Bryan, her financial advisor at the time, which effectively ended any hopes of a reconciliation between the Duke and Duchess. The marriage was ended in divorce on 30 May 1996. The Duke of York spoke fondly of his former wife: "We have managed to work together to bring our children up in a way that few others have been able to and I am extremely grateful to be able to do that."<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Duke_of_York.JPG" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/The_Duke_of_York.JPG/220px-The_Duke_of_York.JPG" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/The_Duke_of_York.JPG/330px-The_Duke_of_York.JPG 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8f/The_Duke_of_York.JPG/440px-The_Duke_of_York.JPG 2x" data-file-width="3844" data-file-height="2563" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Duke_of_York.JPG" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Duke of York riding in the carriage procession at <a href="/wiki/Trooping_the_Colour" title="Trooping the Colour">Trooping the Colour</a>, 16 June 2012</div></div></div>
<p>The couple agreed to share custody of their two daughters, and the Duchess continued to live at the Duke's home, <a href="/wiki/Sunninghill_Park" title="Sunninghill Park">Sunninghill Park</a>, until 2004, when he moved to the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Lodge" title="Royal Lodge">Royal Lodge</a>. In 2003, Richard Kay, in his first gossip column for the <i>Daily Mail</i>, asserted that the Duke was about to marry the businesswoman <a href="/wiki/Amanda_Staveley" title="Amanda Staveley">Amanda Staveley</a>. She was reported in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Telegraph" title="The Sunday Telegraph">The Sunday Telegraph</a></i> as saying, "I will not be marrying Andrew now or in the future." In 2007, Sarah, Duchess of York, purchased Dolphin House, a mansion directly beside the Royal Lodge. In 2008, a fire at Dolphin House resulted in Sarah moving into the Royal Lodge, again sharing a house with the Duke of York. Prince Andrew's lease of <a href="/wiki/Royal_Lodge" title="Royal Lodge">Royal Lodge</a> is for 75 years, with the Crown Estate as landlord, and there is no annual tenancy charge.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2010, Sarah, Duchess of York, was filmed by a <i><a href="/wiki/News_of_the_World" title="News of the World">News of the World</a></i> reporter claiming that her former husband had agreed that if she were to receive ¬£500,000, he would meet the donor and pass on useful top-level business contacts. She was filmed receiving, in cash, $40,000 as a down payment. The Duke's entourage emphatically denied he knew of the situation.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> In July 2011, Sarah stated that her multi-million pound debts had been cleared due to the intervention of her former husband, whom she compared to a "knight on a white charger".<sup id="cite_ref-Teleg_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Teleg-35">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Friendship_with_Jeffrey_Epstein_and_sex_abuse_allegations">Friendship with Jeffrey Epstein and sex abuse allegations</span></h3>
<p>In March 2011, it was reported that the Duke's friendship with <a href="/wiki/Jeffrey_Epstein" title="Jeffrey Epstein">Jeffrey Epstein</a>, an American financier and convicted <a href="/wiki/Sex_offender" title="Sex offender">sex offender</a>, was producing "a steady stream of criticism". Sarah, Duchess of York, disclosed that the Duke helped arrange for Epstein to pay off some of her debts.<sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> The Duke strolled publicly with Epstein after the latter's release from prison, allegedly while negotiating this financial help.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> In July 2011, the Duke was reported to have cut all ties with Epstein,<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> and the Duke's role as Trade Envoy was terminated that month.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2015, there was renewed pressure for Buckingham Palace to explain the Duke's connection with Epstein.<sup id="cite_ref-JonSwaine_40-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JonSwaine-40">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Peter_Oborne" title="Peter Oborne">Peter Oborne</a>, writing in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" title="The Daily Telegraph">The Daily Telegraph</a></i> in January 2015, stated that "the proven facts are grim enough. What was the prince doing, in the first place, with Epstein, a <a href="/wiki/Paedophile" class="mw-redirect" title="Paedophile">paedophile</a> who was jailed in 2008 for soliciting young girls for under-age prostitution?"<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The same month, Virginia Roberts Giuffre made allegations of sexual impropriety against the Duke in court papers related to a <a href="/wiki/Two_Jane_Does_v_US" title="Two Jane Does v US">civil action in Florida</a> arising from her connection to the Epstein case, but to which the Duke was not a party. Roberts claimed that the Duke was among men, including "a former prime minister" and <a href="/wiki/Alan_Dershowitz" title="Alan Dershowitz">Alan Dershowitz</a>, who had sex with her while she was a teenager.<sup id="cite_ref-lied_42-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lied-42">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> She alleged Epstein paid her ¬£10,000 to have sex with the Duke.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> She asserted that she had sex with the Duke on three occasions, including a trip to London in 2001, when she was 17<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> and again in New York and on a private Caribbean island.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup> Flight logs show the Duke and Virginia Roberts were in the places she alleges the sex happened.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> The Duke and Roberts were also photographed together with the Duke's arm round her waist,<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> though Andrew's friends have repeatedly claimed the photo is fake and edited.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> Roberts said she was pressured to have sex with the Duke and "wouldn't have dared object" and feared leaving, as she felt Epstein, through contacts, could have got her "killed or abducted". The allegations have, as of early 2015, not been tested in any court,<sup id="cite_ref-RoyGreenslade_49-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RoyGreenslade-49">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> but Roberts repeated allegations against the Duke and against Epstein in a sworn legal statement under penalty of <a href="/wiki/Perjury#United_States" title="Perjury">perjury</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Buckingham_Palace" title="Buckingham Palace">Buckingham Palace</a> stated that "any suggestion of impropriety with underage minors is categorically untrue", later repeating the denials.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup> Lawyers for Roberts claim a request to the Duke for a statement under oath about the allegations was returned unanswered.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> When the Duke was asked about the allegations by a journalist at the <a href="/wiki/World_Economic_Forum" title="World Economic Forum">World Economic Forum</a>, he refused to answer and left the room.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Dershowitz said, "she's lied about me&#160;... she should not be believed about anyone else&#160;... it must be presumed all her allegations against Prince Andrew were false as well."<sup id="cite_ref-lied_42-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-lied-42">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup> Dershowitz initiated legal proceedings contesting the allegations and he and Epstein are suing the lawyers representing Roberts.<sup id="cite_ref-JonSwaine_40-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-JonSwaine-40">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup> In response Virginia Roberts stated she would not "be bullied back into silence."<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 7 April 2015, Judge <a href="/wiki/Kenneth_Marra" title="Kenneth Marra">Kenneth Marra</a> ruled that the "sex allegations made against Prince Andrew in court papers filed in Florida must be struck from the public record".<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup> Marra made no ruling as to whether claims by Roberts are true or false, specifically stating that Roberts may later give evidence when the case comes to court.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In August 2019, court documents associated with a defamation case, involving <a href="/wiki/Ghislaine_Maxwell" title="Ghislaine Maxwell">Ghislaine Maxwell</a>, revealed that a second girl, Joanna Sjoberg, gave evidence alleging that Prince Andrew had placed his hand on her breast while seated with Roberts in Epstein's mansion while posing for a photo with his <i><a href="/wiki/Spitting_Image" title="Spitting Image">Spitting Image</a></i> puppet.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> Later that month, the Duke released a statement, emphasizing that "At no stage during the limited time I spent with [Epstein] did I see, witness or suspect any behaviour of the sort that subsequently led to his arrest and conviction," though he expressed regret for meeting him in 2010 after Epstein had already pleaded guilty to sex crimes for the first time.<sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id="Trade.2C_business.2C_activities.2C_and_charitable_work"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Trade,_business,_activities,_and_charitable_work">Trade, business, activities, and charitable work</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg/220px-Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="163" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg/330px-Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/d/d2/Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg/440px-Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="890" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Duke_of_York_-_World_Economic_Forum_on_the_Middle_East_2008.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Duke of York in his role as the UK's Special Representative for International Trade and Investment at the <a href="/wiki/World_Economic_Forum" title="World Economic Forum">World Economic Forum</a> on the Middle East, 2008.</div></div></div>
<p>Prince Andrew has been the chairman of the <a href="/wiki/Outward_Bound" title="Outward Bound">Outward Bound Trust</a> since 1999, succeeding his father the Duke of Edinburgh. The charity tries to instil leadership qualities among young people.<sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup> From 2001 until July 2011, the Duke of York worked with <a href="/wiki/UK_Trade_%26_Investment" title="UK Trade &amp; Investment">UK Trade &amp; Investment</a>, part of the <a href="/wiki/Department_for_Business,_Innovation_and_Skills" title="Department for Business, Innovation and Skills">Department for Business, Innovation and Skills</a>, as the United Kingdom's <a href="/wiki/Special_Representative_for_International_Trade_and_Investment" title="Special Representative for International Trade and Investment">Special Representative for International Trade and Investment</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup> The post, previously held by <a href="/wiki/Prince_Edward,_Duke_of_Kent" title="Prince Edward, Duke of Kent">Prince Edward, Duke of Kent</a>, involved representing and promoting the UK at various trade fairs and conferences around the world.<sup id="cite_ref-Trade-ED_7-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Trade-ED-7">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> His suitability for the role was challenged in the <a href="/wiki/House_of_Commons_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="House of Commons of the United Kingdom">House of Commons</a> by Shadow Justice Minister <a href="/wiki/Chris_Bryant" title="Chris Bryant">Chris Bryant</a> in February 2011, at the time of the <a href="/wiki/2011_Libyan_civil_war" class="mw-redirect" title="2011 Libyan civil war">2011 Libyan civil war</a>, on the grounds that he was "not only a very close friend of <a href="/wiki/Saif_al-Islam_Gaddafi" title="Saif al-Islam Gaddafi">Saif al-Islam Gaddafi</a>, but also&#160;... a close friend of the convicted Libyan gun smuggler Tarek Kaituni".<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> The Duke is Patron of the Middle East Association (MEA), the UK's premier organisation for promoting trade and good relations with the Middle East, North Africa, Turkey and Iran.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup>  Since that ended the Duke continued to support UK enterprise without a special role.  <a href="/wiki/Robert_Jobson" title="Robert Jobson">Robert Jobson</a> claims he does this work well and wrote, "He is particularly passionate when dealing with young start-up entrepreneurs and bringing them together with successful businesses at networking and showcasing events.  Andrew is direct and to the point, and his methods seem to work." <sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Duke is also Patron of <a href="/wiki/Fight_for_Sight_(UK)" title="Fight for Sight (UK)">Fight for Sight</a>, a charity dedicated to research into the prevention and treatment of blindness and eye disease,<sup id="cite_ref-68" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-68">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> and was a member of <a href="/wiki/The_Scout_Association" title="The Scout Association">the Scout Association</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He tours Canada frequently to undertake duties related to his Canadian military role. Rick Peters, the former Commanding Officer of <a href="/wiki/The_Royal_Highland_Fusiliers_of_Canada" title="The Royal Highland Fusiliers of Canada">the Royal Highland Fusiliers of Canada</a> stated that Prince Andrew is "very well informed on Canadian military methods."<sup id="cite_ref-70" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-70">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg/220px-Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg/330px-Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg/440px-Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg 2x" data-file-width="500" data-file-height="334" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Dmitry_Medvedev_in_Yuzhno-Sakhalink_18_February_2009-2.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Prince Andrew, Russian President <a href="/wiki/Dmitry_Medvedev" title="Dmitry Medvedev">Medvedev</a> and Japanese PM <a href="/wiki/Tar%C5%8D_As%C5%8D" title="Tar≈ç As≈ç">Tar≈ç As≈ç</a> visit the <a href="/wiki/Sakhalin-II" title="Sakhalin-II">Sakhalin-II</a> oil and gas project in the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Far_East" title="Russian Far East">Russian Far East</a>, 2009</div></div></div>
<p>The Duke of York receives a ¬£249,000 annuity from the Queen.<sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup> <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Times" title="The Sunday Times">The Sunday Times</a></i> reported in July 2008 that for "the Duke of York's public role,... he last year received ¬£436,000 to cover his expenses."<sup id="cite_ref-72" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-72">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> On 8 March 2011, <i><a href="/wiki/The_Daily_Telegraph" title="The Daily Telegraph">The Daily Telegraph</a></i> reported: "In 2010, the Prince spent ¬£620,000 as a trade envoy, including ¬£154,000 on hotels, food and hospitality and ¬£465,000 on travel."<sup id="cite_ref-73" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-73">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>While touring India as a part of the <a href="/wiki/Diamond_Jubilee_of_Queen_Elizabeth_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Diamond Jubilee of Queen Elizabeth II">Queen's Diamond Jubilee</a> in 2012,<sup id="cite_ref-74" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-74">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup> Andrew became interested in the work of Women's Interlink Foundation (WIF), a charity which helps women acquire skills to earn income. He and his family later initiated Key to Freedom, a project which tries to "find a route to market for products made by WIF."<sup id="cite_ref-75" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-75">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup> On 3 September 2012, the Duke of York was among a team of 40 people who abseiled down <a href="/wiki/The_Shard" title="The Shard">The Shard</a> (tallest building in Europe) to raise money for educational charities the Outward Bound Trust and the Royal Marines Charitable Trust Fund.<sup id="cite_ref-77" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-77">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-78" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-78">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In 2013, it was announced that the Duke was becoming the Patron of <a href="/wiki/London_Metropolitan_University" title="London Metropolitan University">London Metropolitan University</a>
<sup id="cite_ref-79" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-79">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Huddersfield" title="University of Huddersfield">University of Huddersfield</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-80" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-80">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-81" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-81">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> In July 2015, he was installed as Chancellor of the University of Huddersfield.<sup id="cite_ref-Huddersfield_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Huddersfield-82">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup> In recognition of the Duke's promotion of entrepreneurship he was elected to an Honorary Fellowship at <a href="/wiki/Hughes_Hall" class="mw-redirect" title="Hughes Hall">Hughes Hall</a> in the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Cambridge" title="University of Cambridge">University of Cambridge</a> on 1 May 2018.<sup id="cite_ref-Hughes_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Hughes-83">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> He became the Patron of the charity Attend<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> in 2003, and is a member of the International Advisory Board of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_United_Services_Institute" title="Royal United Services Institute">Royal United Services Institute</a>.
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg/220px-The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="246" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg/330px-The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5f/The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg/440px-The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1147" data-file-height="1281" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:The_Duke_of_York_in_Belfast.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Duke of York in <a href="/wiki/Titanic_Belfast" title="Titanic Belfast">Titanic Belfast</a> on 29 January 2013</div></div></div>
<p>In 2014, the Duke of York founded the Pitch@Palace initiative<sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> to support entrepreneurs with the amplification and acceleration of their business ideas. Entrepreneurs selected for Pitch@Palace Bootcamp are officially invited by the Duke<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup> to attend St. James Palace in order to pitch their ideas and to be connected with potential investors, mentors and business contacts.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> The Duke has also founded The Prince Andrew Charitable Trust which aims to support young people in different areas such as education and training.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup> He has also founded a number of awards including Inspiring Digital Enterprise Award (iDEA), a programme to develop the digital and enterprise skills,<sup id="cite_ref-89" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-89">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> the Duke of York Award for Technical Education, given to talented young people in technical education,<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> and the Duke of York Young Entrepreneur Award, which recognises talents of young people in entrepreneurship.<sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup> The Duke of York has lent his support to organisations that focus on science and technology by becoming the patron of <a href="/wiki/Catalyst_Inc" title="Catalyst Inc">Catalyst Inc</a> and <a href="/wiki/TeenTech" title="TeenTech">TeenTech</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-96" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-96">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> In 2014, Andrew visited Geneva, Switzerland, to promote British science at <a href="/wiki/CERN" title="CERN">CERN</a>'s 60th anniversary celebrations.<sup id="cite_ref-97" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-97">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup> In May 2018, he visited China and opened the Pitch@Palace China Bootcamp 2.0 at <a href="/wiki/Peking_University" title="Peking University">Peking University</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-98" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-98">&#91;96&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In March 2019, the Duke of York took over the patronage of the <a href="/wiki/Outward_Bound" title="Outward Bound">Outward Bound</a> Trust from his father, the Duke of Edinburgh. Prince Andrew had held the position of chairman of the board of trustees since 1999.<sup id="cite_ref-99" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-99">&#91;97&#93;</a></sup> In May 2019, it was announced that the Duke had succeeded <a href="/wiki/Peter_Carrington" class="mw-redirect" title="Peter Carrington">Peter Carrington</a> as patron of the Royal Fine Art Commission Trust.<sup id="cite_ref-100" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-100">&#91;98&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Politics">Politics</span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_(10224154325).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_%2810224154325%29.jpg/220px-Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_%2810224154325%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_%2810224154325%29.jpg/330px-Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_%2810224154325%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b9/Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_%2810224154325%29.jpg/440px-Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_%2810224154325%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2362" data-file-height="1575" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Hillary_Rodham_Clinton_Prince_Andrew_Chatham_House_Prize_2013_Award_Ceremony_(10224154325).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Hillary_Clinton" title="Hillary Clinton">Hillary Clinton</a> being presented with the 2013 <a href="/wiki/Chatham_House_Prize" class="mw-redirect" title="Chatham House Prize">Chatham House Prize</a> by Prince Andrew</div></div></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_(48000863521).jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_%2848000863521%29.jpg/220px-President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_%2848000863521%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="147" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_%2848000863521%29.jpg/330px-President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_%2848000863521%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e6/President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_%2848000863521%29.jpg/440px-President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_%2848000863521%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2048" data-file-height="1365" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:President_Trump_at_St._James%27s_Palace_(48000863521).jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Prince Andrew with U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> on 4 June 2019</div></div></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Alleged_comments_on_corruption_and_Kazakhstan">Alleged comments on corruption and Kazakhstan</span></h3>
<p>As the United Kingdom's Special Trade Representative, the Duke of York travelled the world to promote British businesses. It was revealed in the <a href="/wiki/United_States_diplomatic_cables_leak" title="United States diplomatic cables leak">United States diplomatic cables leak</a> that the Duke had been reported on by Tatiana Gfoeller, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Ambassador_to_Kyrgyzstan" class="mw-redirect" title="United States Ambassador to Kyrgyzstan">United States Ambassador to Kyrgyzstan</a>, discussing bribery in Kyrgyzstan and the investigation into the <a href="/wiki/Al-Yamamah_arms_deal" title="Al-Yamamah arms deal">Al-Yamamah arms deal</a>. The Duke, she explained, "was referencing an investigation, subsequently closed, into alleged kickbacks a senior Saudi royal had received in exchange for the multi-year, lucrative <a href="/wiki/BAE_Systems" title="BAE Systems">BAE Systems</a> contract to provide equipment and training to Saudi security forces."<sup id="cite_ref-101" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-101">&#91;99&#93;</a></sup> The dispatch continued: "His mother's subjects seated around the table roared their approval. He then went on to 'these (expletive) journalists, especially from <a href="/wiki/The_Guardian" title="The Guardian">the National Guardian</a> &#32;&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Sic" title="Sic">sic</a></i>&#93;, who poke their noses everywhere' and (presumably) make it harder for British businessmen to do business. The crowd practically clapped!"<sup id="cite_ref-102" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-102">&#91;100&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Earlier in 2010, it was revealed that the <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a> President's billionaire son-in-law <a href="/wiki/Timur_Kulibayev" title="Timur Kulibayev">Timur Kulibayev</a> paid the Duke of York's representatives ¬£15 million ‚Äì ¬£3 million over the asking price ‚Äì via offshore companies, for the Duke's <a href="/wiki/Surrey" title="Surrey">Surrey</a> mansion, <a href="/wiki/Sunninghill_Park" title="Sunninghill Park">Sunninghill Park</a>. Kulibayev frequently appears in US dispatches as one of the men who have accumulated millions in gas-rich Kazakhstan.<sup id="cite_ref-103" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-103">&#91;101&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2012, it was reported that Swiss and Italian police investigating "a network of personal and business relationships" allegedly used for "international corruption" were looking at the activities of Enviro Pacific Investments which charges "multi-million pound fees" to energy companies wishing to deal with Kazakhstan.<sup id="cite_ref-sun_104-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sun-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> The trust is believed to have paid ¬£6 million towards the purchase of Sunninghill which now appears derelict.<sup id="cite_ref-sun_104-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sun-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup> In response, a Palace spokesman said "This was a private sale between two trusts. There was never any impropriety on the part of The Duke of York".<sup id="cite_ref-sun_104-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sun-104">&#91;102&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/Libby_Purves" title="Libby Purves">Libby Purves</a> wrote in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Times" title="The Times">The Times</a></i> in January 2015: "Prince Andrew dazzles easily when confronted with immense wealth and apparent power. He has fallen for 'friendships' with bad, corrupt and clever men, not only in the US but in Libya, Kazakhstan, Uzbekistan, Tunisia, wherever."<sup id="cite_ref-RoyGreenslade_49-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-RoyGreenslade-49">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2016, a fresh controversy broke out when the <i>Daily Mail</i> alleged that the Duke had brokered a deal to assist a Greek and Swiss consortium secure a ¬£385 million contract to build water and sewerage networks in two of Kazakhstan's largest cities, while working as British trade envoy, and had stood to gain a ¬£4 million payment in commission.<sup id="cite_ref-105" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-105">&#91;103&#93;</a></sup> The newspaper published an email from the Duke to Kazakh oligarch Kenges Rakishev, (who had allegedly brokered sale of the Prince's Berkshire mansion Sunninghill Park), and claimed that Rakishev had arranged meetings for the consortium. After initially claiming the email was a forgery, Buckingham Palace sought to block its publication as a privacy breach.<sup id="cite_ref-Sawer_106-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sawer-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>   The Palace strongly denied the allegation that the Duke had acted as a "fixer" calling the article "untrue, defamatory and a breach of the editor's code of conduct."<sup id="cite_ref-Sawer_106-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sawer-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>A former Foreign Office minister, MP <a href="/wiki/Chris_Bryant" title="Chris Bryant">Chris Bryant</a> stated: "When I was at the Foreign Office it was very difficult to see in whose interests he [the Duke] was acting. He doesn't exactly add lustre to the Royal diadem."<sup id="cite_ref-Sawer_106-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Sawer-106">&#91;104&#93;</a></sup> There were calls for an official enquiry, the head of campaign group Republic saying "this appears to represent abuse of Andrew's position as trade envoy."<sup id="cite_ref-107" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-107">&#91;105&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Election_to_Royal_Society">Election to Royal Society</span></h3>
<p>Andrew's election to the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Society" title="Royal Society">Royal Society</a> prompted "Britain's leading scientists" to "revolt" due to Andrew's lack of scientific background, with some noting he had only a secondary school level education.<sup id="cite_ref-sunday_108-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sunday-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup> In an <a href="/wiki/Op-ed" title="Op-ed">op-ed</a> in <i><a href="/wiki/The_Sunday_Times" title="The Sunday Times">The Sunday Times</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Humboldt_Prize" title="Humboldt Prize">Humboldt Prize</a> recipient <a href="/wiki/David_Colquhoun" title="David Colquhoun">David Colquhoun</a> opined, in references to Andrew's qualifications, that "if I wanted a tip for the winner of the 14.30 at <a href="/wiki/Newmarket_Racecourse" title="Newmarket Racecourse">Newmarket</a>, I‚Äôd ask a royal. For most other questions, I wouldn‚Äôt."<sup id="cite_ref-sunday_108-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sunday-108">&#91;106&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-109" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-109">&#91;107&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Meetings_with_Ilham_Aliyev">Meetings with Ilham Aliyev</span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain,_Prince_Andrew.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain%2C_Prince_Andrew.jpg/220px-Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain%2C_Prince_Andrew.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="175" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain%2C_Prince_Andrew.jpg/330px-Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain%2C_Prince_Andrew.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/05/Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain%2C_Prince_Andrew.jpg/440px-Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain%2C_Prince_Andrew.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1285" data-file-height="1020" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ilham_Aliyev_met_with_Duke_of_York_of_the_Great_Britain,_Prince_Andrew.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>The Duke of York with <a href="/wiki/Ilham_Aliyev" title="Ilham Aliyev">Ilham Aliyev</a></div></div></div>
<p>As of November 2014, the Duke had met <a href="/wiki/Ilham_Aliyev" title="Ilham Aliyev">Ilham Aliyev</a>, the president of <a href="/wiki/Azerbaijan" title="Azerbaijan">Azerbaijan</a>, on 12 separate occasions.<sup id="cite_ref-Independent_110-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Independent-110">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>  He had to stand down as a trade envoy for the UK in 2011 following controversy over his friendship with Aliyev, who has been criticised for corruption and for abuses of human rights by <a href="/wiki/Amnesty_International" title="Amnesty International">Amnesty International</a>, but he has continued to visit him in Azerbaijan since standing down.<sup id="cite_ref-Independent_110-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Independent-110">&#91;108&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arms_sales">Arms sales</span></h3>
<p>In March 2011, Kaye Stearman of the <a href="/wiki/Campaign_Against_the_Arms_Trade" class="mw-redirect" title="Campaign Against the Arms Trade">Campaign Against the Arms Trade</a> told <a href="/wiki/Channel_4_News" title="Channel 4 News">Channel 4 News</a> CAAT sees Prince Andrew as part of a bigger problem, "He is the front man for <a href="/wiki/UK_Trade_%26_Investment" title="UK Trade &amp; Investment">UKTI</a>. Our concerns are not just Prince Andrew, it's the whole UKTI set up. They see arms as just another commodity but it has completely disproportionate resources. At the London office of UKTI the arms sector has more staff than all the others put together.  We are concerned that Prince Andrew is used to sell arms, and where you sell arms it is likely to be to despotic regimes. He is the cheerleader in chief for the arms industry, shaking hands and paving the way for the salesmen."<sup id="cite_ref-111" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-111">&#91;109&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In January 2014, Prince Andrew took part in a delegation to <a href="/wiki/Bahrain" title="Bahrain">Bahrain</a>, a close ally of the United Kingdom. Spokesman for CAAT, Andrew Smith said, "We are calling on Prince Andrew and the UK government to stop selling arms to Bahrain. By endorsing the <a href="/wiki/Human_rights_in_Bahrain" title="Human rights in Bahrain">Bahraini dictatorship</a> Prince Andrew is giving his implicit support to their oppressive practices.  When our government sells arms it is giving moral and practical support to an illegitimate and authoritarian regime and directly supporting their systematic crackdown on opposition groups. (...) We shouldn't allow our international image to be used as a PR tool for the violent and oppressive dictatorship in Bahrain."<sup id="cite_ref-112" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-112">&#91;110&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Andrew Smith has also said, "The prince has consistently used his position to promote arms sales and boost some of the most unpleasant governments in the world, his arms sales haven‚Äôt just given military support to corrupt and repressive regimes. They've lent those regimes political and international legitimacy."<sup id="cite_ref-113" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-113">&#91;111&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_interests">Personal interests</span></h2>
<p>The Duke is a capable <a href="/wiki/Golf" title="Golf">golfer</a>, playing off a low single-figure <a href="/wiki/Handicap_(golf)" title="Handicap (golf)">handicap</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-114" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-114">&#91;112&#93;</a></sup> He was Captain of the <a href="/wiki/Royal_and_Ancient_Golf_Club_of_St_Andrews" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal and Ancient Golf Club of St Andrews">Royal and Ancient Golf Club of St Andrews</a> between 2003 and 2004‚Äîduring the club's 250th anniversary season‚Äîis patron of a number of royal golf clubs, and has been elected as an honorary member of many others. The Duke is also a keen <a href="/wiki/Skiing" title="Skiing">skier</a> and has bought an exclusive skiing chalet in <a href="/wiki/Verbier" title="Verbier">Verbier</a>, <a href="/wiki/Switzerland" title="Switzerland">Switzerland</a>, for between ¬£8 million and ¬£13 million jointly with Sarah Ferguson.<sup id="cite_ref-115" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-115">&#91;113&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>The Duke is a <a href="/wiki/Liveryman" class="mw-redirect" title="Liveryman">Liveryman</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Worshipful_Company_of_Shipwrights" title="Worshipful Company of Shipwrights">Worshipful Company of Shipwrights</a>, the senior maritime <a href="/wiki/City_of_London" title="City of London">City</a> livery company.<sup id="cite_ref-116" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-116">&#91;114&#93;</a></sup> In May 2008, he attended a goose-hunt in Kazakhstan with President <a href="/wiki/Nursultan_Nazarbayev" title="Nursultan Nazarbayev">Nursultan Nazarbayev</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-117" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-117">&#91;115&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span id="Titles.2C_styles.2C_honours_and_arms"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Titles,_styles,_honours_and_arms">Titles, styles, honours and arms</span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Titles_and_styles">Titles and styles</span></h3>
<ul><li>1960‚Äì1986: His Royal Highness The Prince Andrew<sup id="cite_ref-Titles_118-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Titles-118">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup></li>
<li>1986‚Äìpresent: His Royal Highness The Duke of York</li></ul>
<p>Andrew is currently the eighth in the line of succession to the throne.<sup id="cite_ref-119" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-119">&#91;117&#93;</a></sup> He is known by his secondary titles of Earl of Inverness in <a href="/wiki/Inverness" title="Inverness">Inverness</a> and Baron Killyleagh in <a href="/wiki/Killyleagh" title="Killyleagh">Killyleagh</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Titles_118-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Titles-118">&#91;116&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Naval_ranks">Naval ranks</span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a></span> 1979‚Äì1981: <a href="/wiki/Midshipman" title="Midshipman">Midshipman</a>, <a href="/wiki/Britannia_Royal_Naval_College" title="Britannia Royal Naval College">Britannia Royal Naval College</a>, <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Culdrose_(HMS_Seahawk)" title="RNAS Culdrose (HMS Seahawk)">HMS <i>Seahawk</i></a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a></span> 1981‚Äì1984: <a href="/wiki/Sub_Lieutenant" class="mw-redirect" title="Sub Lieutenant">Sub Lieutenant</a>, Pilot, 820 NAS on <a href="/wiki/HMS_Invincible_(R05)" title="HMS Invincible (R05)">HMS <i>Invincible</i></a>;</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a></span> 1984‚Äì1992: <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant" title="Lieutenant">Lieutenant</a>, Pilot, 815 NAS on <a href="/wiki/HMS_Brazen_(F91)" title="HMS Brazen (F91)">HMS <i>Brazen</i></a>; Helicopter Warfare Instructor, 702 NAS at RNAS Culdrose; Flight Commander, 829 NAS on <a href="/wiki/HMS_Campbeltown_(F86)" title="HMS Campbeltown (F86)">HMS <i>Campbeltown</i></a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a></span> 1992‚Äì1999: <a href="/wiki/Lieutenant_Commander" class="mw-redirect" title="Lieutenant Commander">Lieutenant Commander</a>, Captain, <a href="/wiki/HMS_Cottesmore_(M32)" title="HMS Cottesmore (M32)">HMS <i>Cottesmore</i></a>; Senior Pilot, 815 NAS at <a href="/wiki/RNAS_Portland" class="mw-redirect" title="RNAS Portland">RNAS Portland</a>; Directorate of Naval Operations, <a href="/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_(United_Kingdom)" title="Ministry of Defence (United Kingdom)">British Ministry of Defence</a></li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a></span> 1999‚Äì2005: <a href="/wiki/Commander_(Royal_Navy)" title="Commander (Royal Navy)">Commander</a>, Diplomacy Section of the Naval Staff</li>
<li><span class="flagicon"><a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/23px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="12" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/35px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9c/Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg/46px-Naval_Ensign_of_the_United_Kingdom.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="720" data-file-height="360" /></a></span> 2005‚Äì2010: <a href="/wiki/Captain_(Royal_Navy)" title="Captain (Royal Navy)">Captain</a></li>
