<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Arms">Arms</span></h3>
<table class="wikitable collapsible" style="width: 100%">
<caption>Coat of arms of the Duke of York
</caption>
<tbody><tr>
<td style="width: 220px; min-width:220px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew,_Duke_of_York.svg" class="image"><img alt="Coat of Arms of Andrew, Duke of York.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg/220px-Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="206" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg/330px-Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/74/Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg/440px-Coat_of_Arms_of_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1530" data-file-height="1430" /></a>
</td>
<td>
<dl><dt>Notes</dt>
<dd>The Duke's personal <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms" title="Coat of arms">coat of arms</a> are the <a href="/wiki/Royal_coat_of_arms_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Royal coat of arms of the United Kingdom">Royal coat of arms of the United Kingdom</a> differenced by a label of three points Argent, the central point charged with an anchor Azure.</dd>
<dt>Adopted</dt>
<dd>1963</dd>
<dt>Coronet</dt>
<dd>The <a href="/wiki/Coronet" title="Coronet">coronet</a> of a son of the sovereign Proper, thereon a lion statant guardant Or crowned of the same coronet charged with a label as in the arms.</dd>
<dt>Escutcheon</dt>
<dd>Quarterly 1st and 4th Gules three lions passant guardant in pale Or 2nd Or a lion rampant Gules within a double tressure flory counterflory Gules 3rd Azure a harp Or stringed Argent</dd>
<dt>Supporters</dt>
<dd>Dexter a lion rampant guardant Or imperially crowned proper, sinister a unicorn Argent, armed, crined and unguled Or, gorged with a coronet Or composed of crosses pat√©e and fleurs de lis a chain affixed thereto passing between the forelegs and reflexed over the back also Or.</dd>
<dt>Motto</dt>
<dd>The <a href="/wiki/Order_of_the_Garter" title="Order of the Garter">Order of the Garter</a> ribbon.<br /><b><a href="/wiki/Honi_soit_qui_mal_y_pense" title="Honi soit qui mal y pense">Honi soit qui mal y pense</a></b><br /><i>(Shame be to him who thinks evil of it)</i></dd>
<dt>Other elements</dt>
<dd>The whole differenced by a label of three points Argent, the central point charged with an anchor Azure.</dd>
<dt>Banner</dt>
<dd><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew,_Duke_of_York.svg" class="image"><img alt="Royal Standard of Prince Andrew, Duke of York.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg/50px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="25" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg/75px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c7/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg/100px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500" /></a> The <a href="/wiki/Royal_Standard_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Royal Standard of the United Kingdom">Royal Standard of the United Kingdom</a>, labelled for difference as in his arms. (In Scotland: <a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew,_Earl_of_Inverness.svg" class="image"><img alt="Royal Standard of Prince Andrew, Earl of Inverness.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Earl_of_Inverness.svg/50px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Earl_of_Inverness.svg.png" decoding="async" width="50" height="25" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Earl_of_Inverness.svg/75px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Earl_of_Inverness.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/91/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Earl_of_Inverness.svg/100px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Earl_of_Inverness.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1000" data-file-height="500" /></a>)</dd>
<dt>Symbolism</dt>
<dd>As with the Royal Arms of the United Kingdom. The first and fourth quarters are the arms of <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_England" class="mw-redirect" title="Coat of arms of England">England</a>, the second of <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Scotland" class="mw-redirect" title="Coat of arms of Scotland">Scotland</a>, the third of <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Ireland" title="Coat of arms of Ireland">Ireland</a>. The anchor has been a <a href="/wiki/Cadency" title="Cadency">brisure</a> for Dukes of York since 1892.</dd></dl>
</td></tr></tbody></table>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_flag_for_Canada">Personal flag for Canada</span></h3>
<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Royal_standards_of_Canada#Other_members_of_the_Royal_Family" title="Royal standards of Canada">The Duke of York's Personal Canadian Flag</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew,_Duke_of_York_(in_Canada).svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York_%28in_Canada%29.svg/220px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York_%28in_Canada%29.svg.png" decoding="async" width="220" height="110" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York_%28in_Canada%29.svg/330px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York_%28in_Canada%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/57/Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York_%28in_Canada%29.svg/440px-Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew%2C_Duke_of_York_%28in_Canada%29.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1200" data-file-height="600" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Royal_Standard_of_Prince_Andrew,_Duke_of_York_(in_Canada).svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Flag of the Duke of York for use in Canada</div></div></div>
<p>Since 2014, the Duke of York has a personal <a href="/wiki/Heraldic_flag" title="Heraldic flag">heraldic flag</a> for use in Canada. It is the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Arms_of_Canada" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Arms of Canada">Royal Arms of Canada</a> in <a href="/wiki/Banner_of_arms" title="Banner of arms">banner form</a> defaced with a blue <a href="/wiki/Roundel_(heraldry)" title="Roundel (heraldry)">roundel</a> surrounded by a wreath of gold maple leaves, within which is a depiction of an <i>"A"</i> surmounted by a coronet. Above the roundel is a white <a href="/wiki/Label_(heraldry)" title="Label (heraldry)">label</a> of three points, the centre one charged with an anchor.<sup id="cite_ref-134" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-134">&#91;132&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-135" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-135">&#91;133&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Postage_stamps">Postage stamps</span></h2>
<p>Appears on two stamps with <a href="/wiki/HMS_Herald_(H138)" title="HMS Herald (H138)">HMS <i>Herald</i></a>, issued by <a href="/wiki/Saint_Helena" title="Saint Helena">Saint Helena</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-shipstamps_136-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-shipstamps-136">&#91;134&#93;</a></sup>
</p>

<li id="cite_note-2"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-2">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">Andrew does not usually use a surname but when one is needed, it is <a href="/wiki/Mountbatten-Windsor" title="Mountbatten-Windsor">Mountbatten-Windsor</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
<li id="cite_note-5"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-5">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">His godparents were: <a href="/wiki/Prince_Henry,_Duke_of_Gloucester" title="Prince Henry, Duke of Gloucester">the Duke of Gloucester</a> (his maternal great-uncle); <a href="/wiki/Princess_Alexandra,_The_Honourable_Lady_Ogilvy" title="Princess Alexandra, The Honourable Lady Ogilvy">Princess Alexandra of Kent</a> (his first cousin once removed); <a href="/wiki/Hugh_FitzRoy,_11th_Duke_of_Grafton" title="Hugh FitzRoy, 11th Duke of Grafton">Hugh Fitzroy, Earl Euston</a>, as he then was; the <a href="/wiki/John_Elphinstone,_17th_Lord_Elphinstone" title="John Elphinstone, 17th Lord Elphinstone">Lord Elphinstone</a> (his first cousin once removed); and <a href="/wiki/Georgina_Kennard" title="Georgina Kennard">Mrs Harold Phillips</a> (later Lady Kennard).<sup id="cite_ref-Yvonne_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Yvonne-4">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></span>
</li>
</ol></div></div>
